SELECT [c].[Nome], [c].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Nome], [t0].[Preco], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[Nome0], [t0].[Preco0], [t0].[Id00]
FROM [Categorias] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Nome], [p].[Preco], [t].[Id] AS [Id0], [t].[Nome] AS [Nome0], [t].[Preco] AS [Preco0], [t].[Id0] AS [Id00], [p].[CategoriaId]
    FROM [Produtos] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[Nome], [a].[Preco], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[ProdutoId]
